20#include <stdint.h>
21
22#include <jis0212.h>
23
24/* The defined JIS 0201 positions contains large gaps. It's better to
25 avoid using one large table with such big gaps. Instead we match each
26 char in a table resulting in an index to a table with the UCS. The
27 following command can be used to generate the table:
28
29 egrep '^0x[[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]' \
30 .../eastasia/jis/jis0212.txt | perl tab.pl
31
32 where tab.pl is
33
34 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
35 $first=$last=$idx=0;
36 while (<>) {
37 local($jis,$ucs,%rest) = split;
38 local($u)=hex($ucs);
39 local($j)=hex($jis);
40 local($k) = int(($j - 0x2121) / 256) * 94 + (($j - 0x2121) % 256);
41 if ($k - $last > 6) {
42 if ($last != 0) {
43 printf (" { .start = %#06x, .end = %#06x, .idx = %5d },\n",
44 $first, $last, $idx);
45 $idx += $last - $first + 1;
46 }
47 $first=$k;
48 }
49 $last=$k;
50 }
51 printf (" { .start = %#06x, .end = %#06x, .idx = %5d }\n",
52 $first, $last, $idx);
53 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
54*/
55const struct jisx0212_idx __jisx0212_to_ucs_idx[] =
56{
57 { .start = 0x006c, .end = 0x0076, .idx = 0 },
58 { .start = 0x007f, .end = 0x0081, .idx = 11 },
59 { .start = 0x00a8, .end = 0x00ae, .idx = 14 },
60 { .start = 0x0216, .end = 0x0231, .idx = 21 },
61 { .start = 0x0255, .end = 0x0261, .idx = 49 },
62 { .start = 0x0285, .end = 0x0291, .idx = 62 },
63 { .start = 0x02f0, .end = 0x02ff, .idx = 75 },
64 { .start = 0x0310, .end = 0x031f, .idx = 91 },
65 { .start = 0x034e, .end = 0x03a4, .idx = 107 },
66 { .start = 0x03ac, .end = 0x0402, .idx = 194 },
67 { .start = 0x0582, .end = 0x1c2a, .idx = 281 },
68 { .start = 0xffff, .end = 0xffff, .idx = 0 },
69};
70
71
72/* The table which the UCS values indexed by the table above can be
73 generated using the following code:
74
75 egrep '^0x[[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]' \
76 .../eastasia/jis/jis0212.txt | perl tab.pl
77
78 where tab.pl is:
79
80 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
81 $first=$last=$idx=0;
82
83 sub fmt {
84 printf ("\n ") if (($n % 8) == 0);
85 ++$n;
86 my($val) = pop(@_);
87 printf (" %#06x,", $val);
88 }
89
90 while (<>) {
91 local($jis,$ucs,%rest) = split;
92 local($u)=hex($ucs);
93 local($j)=hex($jis);
94 local($k) = int(($j - 0x2121) / 256) * 94 + (($j - 0x2121) % 256);
95 if ($k - $last > 6) {
96 if ($last != 0) {
97 $idx += $last - $first + 1;
98 }
99 $first=$k;
100 } else {
101 for ($m = $last + 1; $m < $k; ++$m) {
102 fmt (0);
103 }
104 }
105 fmt ($u);
106 $last=$k;
107 }
108 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
109*/

876/* The UCS char covered by JIS X0212 are sparsely distributed. So we
877 use again a two-step mapping table. The index table can be computed
878 using
879
880 egrep '^0x[[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]' \
881 ../eastasia/jis/jis0212.txt | awk '{ print $2, $1 }' | sort -u |
882 perl tab.pl
883
884 where tab.pl is
885
886 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
887 $first=$last=$idx=0;
888 while (<>) {
889 local($ucs,$jis,%rest) = split;
890 local($u)=hex($ucs);
891 local($j)=hex($jis);
892 if ($u - $last > 6) {
893 if ($last != 0) {
894 printf (" { .start = %#06x, .end = %#06x, .idx = %5d },\n",
895 $first, $last, $idx);
896 $idx += $last - $first + 1;
897 }
898 $first=$u;
899 }
900 $last=$u;
901 }
902 printf (" { .start = %#06x, .end = %#06x, .idx = %5d }, \n",
903 $first, $last, $idx);
904 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
905*/
906const struct jisx0212_idx __jisx0212_from_ucs_idx[] =
907{

1659/* The values corresponding to the table can be computed using
1660
1661 egrep '^0x[[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]' \
1662 .../eastasia/jis/jis0212.txt | awk '{ print $2, $1 }' |
1663 sort -u | perl tab.pl
1664
1665 where tab.pl contains:
1666
1667 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1668 $first=$last=$idx=0;
1669
1670 sub fmt {
1671 printf ("\n ") if (($n % 6) == 0);
1672 ++$n;
1673 my($val) = pop(@_);
1674 printf (" \"\\x%02x\\x%02x\",",
1675 $val < 256 ? $val : int($val / 256),
1676 $val < 256 ? 0 : $val % 256);
1677 }
1678
1679 while (<>) {
1680 local($ucs,$jis,%rest) = split;
1681 local($u)=hex($ucs);
1682 local($j)=hex($jis);
1683 if ($u - $last > 6) {
1684 if ($last != 0) {
1685 $idx += $last - $first + 1;
1686 }
1687 $first=$u;
1688 } else {
1689 for ($m = $last + 1; $m < $u; ++$m) {
1690 fmt (0);
1691 }
1692 }
1693 fmt ($j);
1694 $last=$u;
1695 }
1696 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1697*/
